【内容】:
Neural Radiance Fields (NeRF) and 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) have demonstrated strong capability in reconstructing 3D scenes ranging from indoor to outdoor environments. For large- scale scenes, reconstruction is often accelerated through paral- lelization based on geographic partitioning. However, excessive scene size introduces viewpoint locality, leading to two major chal- lenges: reconstruction isolation and redundant computation. The former causes significant inconsistency in rendering quality across viewpoints and the latter leads to repetitive optimization of similar elements, resulting in wasted computational resources. Inspired by the expert optimization principle in Mixture-of-Experts (MoEs), we propose EGGS (Expert-Guided Framework Constructed from Semantic Priors for Large-Scale Scene Reconstruction), an expert- guided framework that replaces geographic partitioning with ex- pert collaboration constructed from semantic priors. EGGS as- signs experts to scene elements based on semantic and feature similarity, enabling semantic-aware collaboration that effectively

【内容】:
First, Reconstruction Isolation. Each subregion reconstruc- tion relies on the viewpoints that observe its internal content. Since viewpoints only provide limited coverage within individ- ual regions, reconstruction quality varies significantly across sub- regions, an issue unique to large-scale reconstruction. Recent work [20] attempts to improve inter-region consistency via addi- tional loss constraints, yet viewpoint locality remains unresolved: high-quality subregions fail to enhance adjacent low-quality ones, ultimately degrading overall reconstruction fidelity.

【内容】:
Second, Redundant Computation. Geographic partition- ing separates semantic entities such as buildings, vegetation, and roads; due to viewpoint locality, these elements are repeatedly “rediscovered” and “relearned”. This scheme overlooks seman- tic and structural redundancy, causing repetitive subregion recon- structions that raise computational costs and reduce overall recon- struction quality.

Third, Multi-Expert Collaboration and Competition. Modular-GS [34] introduce MoEs [31] into 3DGS for semantic space decomposition. Inspired by the expert division strategy in MOEs for 3D reconstruction, we propose that an expert-guided structure can go beyond semantic segmentation and serve as an alternative to geographic partitioning. However, the multi-experts structure naturally involves expert competition and cooperation, which necessitates designing collaborative mechanisms to prevent boundary ambiguity that could impair rendering quality.

【元数据】:

【内容】:
To address these challenges, we present EGGS, an Expert- Guided Framework Constructed from Semantic Priors for Large- Scale Scene Reconstruction, which replaces geographic partition- ing with a semantic prior multi-expert guided framework. EGGS significantly improves reconstruction balance across large-scale scenes and reducing computational cost for higher-quality recon- struction across the whole scene. At its core, EGGS leverages an expert-guided strategy to balance and accelerate scene recon- struction through three key parts: First, semantic segmentation di- vides the scene into multiple categories, each assigned to a cat- egory expert trained with semantically rich viewpoints for corre- sponding instance learning and reconstruction. Second, category experts further guide the reconstruction of unselected viewpoints, mitigating reconstruction isolation caused by viewpoint locality and achieving balanced, efficient reconstruction. Third, a collab- orative and constraint-based mechanism promotes expert cooper- ation and suppresses inter-expert conflicts, alleviating boundary- induced blurring.

2.1. Large-scale Scene Reconstruction

--- Element 31 [页码: 2 | 类型: NarrativeText] ---
【元数据】:
  - source: D:\PycharmProject\LLM_Parser\PDF\Shadow\32953_EGGS_Expert_Guided_Frame.pdf
  - coordinates: {'points': ((np.float64(881.0), np.float64(614.0)), (np.float64(881.0), np.float64(940.0)), (np.float64(1537.0), np.float64(940.0)), (np.float64(1537.0), np.float64(614.0))), 'system': 'PixelSpace', 'layout_width': 1700, 'layout_height': 2200}
  - filetype: application/pdf
  - languages: ['eng']
  - last_modified: 2025-12-21T20:38:27
  - page_number: 2
  - file_directory: D:\PycharmProject\LLM_Parser\PDF\Shadow
  - filename: 32953_EGGS_Expert_Guided_Frame.pdf
  - parent_id: 496d5ad8fe1373a444389791616c4dd5
  - category: NarrativeText
  - element_id: 14d3e79eee880fa98c136e57841d6b70
【内容】:
The conflict between high reconstruction costs and low accuracy in large-scale scene reconstruction, driven by scene complexity, re- mains a key challenge in 3D reconstruction. Recent NeRF variants using heuristic partitioning [38, 39, 44] or voxel grids [2, 6, 26, 45] have supported performance in large-scale scenes but are lim- ited by long training times. Alternatively, 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) has introduced methods like progressive [14, 17, 49] and level-of-detail (LOD) schemes [21, 30] to balance quality and ef- ficiency. However, these geographically partitioned methods still suffer from inconsistent reconstruction quality due to viewpoint limitations, leading to degraded overall results.

2.2. Semantic-awareness

--- Element 33 [页码: 2 | 类型: NarrativeText] ---
【元数据】:
  - source: D:\PycharmProject\LLM_Parser\PDF\Shadow\32953_EGGS_Expert_Guided_Frame.pdf
  - coordinates: {'points': ((np.float64(882.0), np.float64(1015.0)), (np.float64(882.0), np.float64(1432.0)), (np.float64(1538.0), np.float64(1432.0)), (np.float64(1538.0), np.float64(1015.0))), 'system': 'PixelSpace', 'layout_width': 1700, 'layout_height': 2200}
  - filetype: application/pdf
  - languages: ['eng']
  - last_modified: 2025-12-21T20:38:27
  - page_number: 2
  - file_directory: D:\PycharmProject\LLM_Parser\PDF\Shadow
  - filename: 32953_EGGS_Expert_Guided_Frame.pdf
  - parent_id: ea9cd456681ad067774dee6cd2669acc
  - category: NarrativeText
  - element_id: 0bbef49634862daba581a6dae74b4fcb
【内容】:
With advancements in 2D semantic understanding [15, 29], recent research has explored semantic integration in 3D reconstruction [3, 8, 28, 47]. Some methods embed semantic information into explicit 3D Gaussian representations by projecting 2D semantic features or aggregating semantic pools [7]. Others leverage ex- ternal semantic models to guide 3DGS training or inference [51], such as introducing semantic viewpoints consistency losses to mit- igate overfitting [11, 41]. These efforts highlight the potential of semantic-aware methods in 3D reconstruction [27], yet their appli- cation in complex, large-scale scenes requires further exploration. Inspired by the growing field of 3D spatial semantic awareness, we aim to leverage rich semantic information in large-scale scenes to overcome viewpoint limitations and enable optimization regard- less of spatial distance.

MoEs framework [10, 12, 35]enables parallel training through ex- pert specialization. Recent successes in visual imaging [31, 46] have inspired its application in 3D reconstruction. Existing work has combined MoEs with 3D reconstruction [4, 5, 19, 34] and made improvements for large-scale scenes [24, 50]. However, prior works have largely ignored the role of experts as reusable semantic priors capable of guiding similar objects that frequently appear in large-scale scenes.

【内容】:
3.1. Overview

--- Element 73 [页码: 3 | 类型: NarrativeText] ---
【元数据】:
  - source: D:\PycharmProject\LLM_Parser\PDF\Shadow\32953_EGGS_Expert_Guided_Frame.pdf
  - coordinates: {'points': ((np.float64(163.0), np.float64(1014.0)), (np.float64(163.0), np.float64(1244.0)), (np.float64(818.0), np.float64(1244.0)), (np.float64(818.0), np.float64(1014.0))), 'system': 'PixelSpace', 'layout_width': 1700, 'layout_height': 2200}
  - filetype: application/pdf
  - languages: ['eng']
  - last_modified: 2025-12-21T20:38:27
  - page_number: 3
  - file_directory: D:\PycharmProject\LLM_Parser\PDF\Shadow
  - filename: 32953_EGGS_Expert_Guided_Frame.pdf
  - parent_id: 8bcda8c4e9721b06bfd0d10aac07b802
  - category: NarrativeText
  - element_id: 3aca10f711ff9ffd8743e919fbfc3b78
【内容】:
EGGS is a large-scale collaborative reconstruction framework based on a semantic partitioned multi-expert model. Instead of dividing scenes into geographic blocks, EGGS establishes a complete reconstruction pipeline through two major systems: an expert-guided framework and expert collaborative reconstruction. These correspond to three key modules: Semantic-Prior Filter- ing, Expert Division & Guidance and Expert Collaborative Re- construction.

--- Element 74 [页码: 3 | 类型: NarrativeText] ---
【元数据】:
  - source: D:\PycharmProject\LLM_Parser\PDF\Shadow\32953_EGGS_Expert_Guided_Frame.pdf
  - coordinates: {'points': ((np.float64(163.0), np.float64(1257.0)), (np.float64(163.0), np.float64(1462.0)), (np.float64(818.0), np.float64(1462.0)), (np.float64(818.0), np.float64(1257.0))), 'system': 'PixelSpace', 'layout_width': 1700, 'layout_height': 2200}
  - filetype: application/pdf
  - languages: ['eng']
  - last_modified: 2025-12-21T20:38:27
  - page_number: 3
  - file_directory: D:\PycharmProject\LLM_Parser\PDF\Shadow
  - filename: 32953_EGGS_Expert_Guided_Frame.pdf
  - parent_id: 8bcda8c4e9721b06bfd0d10aac07b802
  - category: NarrativeText
  - element_id: 11e82a05677f8283cdc57f22c2d32d13
【内容】:
The semantic prior filtering module employs a dual filtering mechanism based on semantics and clustering to select viewpoints and corresponding point clouds that are semantically rich and ex- hibit strong multi-view consistency from large-scale scenes. These selected viewpoints are prioritized during reconstruction, produc- ing high-quality Gaussian anchors that form category-specific ex- perts representing different semantic classes.

--- Element 75 [页码: 3 | 类型: NarrativeText] ---
【元数据】:
  - source: D:\PycharmProject\LLM_Parser\PDF\Shadow\32953_EGGS_Expert_Guided_Frame.pdf
  - coordinates: {'points': ((np.float64(163.0), np.float64(1470.0)), (np.float64(163.0), np.float64(1797.0)), (np.float64(818.0), np.float64(1797.0)), (np.float64(818.0), np.float64(1470.0))), 'system': 'PixelSpace', 'layout_width': 1700, 'layout_height': 2200}
  - filetype: application/pdf
  - languages: ['eng']
  - last_modified: 2025-12-21T20:38:27
  - page_number: 3
  - file_directory: D:\PycharmProject\LLM_Parser\PDF\Shadow
  - filename: 32953_EGGS_Expert_Guided_Frame.pdf
  - parent_id: 8bcda8c4e9721b06bfd0d10aac07b802
  - category: NarrativeText
  - element_id: 91913caa1876be0c78c07957d64ff31b
【内容】:
The expert-guided reconstruction module treats these experts as reconstruction priors. During the preliminary reconstruction stage, EGGS performs stable matching between experts and spa- tially scattered yet semantically consistent elements across the scene, enabling one-to-one expert guidance. Through a graph neu- ral network, prior knowledge is propagated from experts to guide the reconstruction of these elements, achieving high-quality and balanced results. This design effectively mitigates the reconstruc- tion quality disparity and redundant computation “rediscovered” and “relearned”) caused by viewpoint locality and isolated render- ing of repeated structures.

3.2.1. Semantic-Prior Filtering.

--- Element 80 [页码: 3 | 类型: NarrativeText] ---
【元数据】:
  - source: D:\PycharmProject\LLM_Parser\PDF\Shadow\32953_EGGS_Expert_Guided_Frame.pdf

  - file_directory: D:\PycharmProject\LLM_Parser\PDF\Shadow

  - category: NarrativeText
  - element_id: 4741a6bbd3f149609df7b34f4acd47f7
【内容】:
Semantic-prior filtering module of EGGS takes camera view- points, point clouds, and semantic segmentation mas s input to generate a subset of viewpoints and point clouds prioritized for ex- pert reconstruction. This module incorporates a Segmented-Prior filtering mechanism consisting of Segmented Filter and viewpoint clustering. The semantic segmentation mask prior is obtained us- ing the CLIP+SAM[15, 29] model guided by textual prompts to capture semantic regions, as detailed in the supplementary mate- rial, including model parameters and settings. Semantic score fil- tering selects the viewpoints and point clouds that best represent expert-specific reconstruction regions, while viewpoint clustering ensures viewpoints consistency within each expert model.

【内容】:
Step 1: Segmented Filter. To quantify the scene informa- tion richness of all semantic categories within each viewpoint and prioritize viewpoints that capture more structural details for high- quality expert reconstruction, we define the semantic score as a measure of the semantic richness captured by a single viewpoint. This score is computed through the interaction between the 3D point cloud constructed via SfM[33] and the semantic masks asso- ciated with each viewpoint.

Step 2: Viewpoint Clustering. Relying solely on semantic richness to select viewpoints and point clouds for expert recon- struction may compromise viewpoints consistency, leading to se- vere viewpoint locality issues. To address this, we introduce an additional viewpoint clustering stage based on the K-Means al- gorithm, which partitions all viewpoints into multiple clusters ac- cording to their camera parameters.

【内容】:
Expert Construction. The reconstruction isolation and redundant computation issues caused by viewpoint locality essentially stem from the absence of a unified global paradigm to guide and con- strain reconstruction across spatially distributed objects. Under limited viewpoint coverage, identical structures cannot be consis- tently captured from a global perspective, resulting in fragmented reconstructions.

【内容】:
To address this, EGGS constructs multiple category-specific experts using the semantically rich viewpoints and correspond- ing point clouds obtained from the semantic prior filtering mod- ule. These selected data are first reconstructed through a priority reconstruction process, generating high-quality Gaussian anchors that serve as the foundation of each expert. Each category expert is composed of Gaussian anchors corresponding to its semantic cat- egory and acts as a global prior to guide consistent reconstruction across the entire scene, as illustrated in Fig. 2.

Stage 1: Multi-Scale Stable Matching. The stable matching algorithm connects the multi-category experts obtained from pri- ority reconstruction with their corresponding semantic instances across the scene, regardless of geographic separation. By estab- lishing associations purely based on feature similarity rather than spatial proximity, this process eliminates reconstruction isolation caused by inconsistent reconstruction of semantically identical ob- jects distributed across large-scale scenes.

Considering that the classical stable matching algorithm has a computational complexity of O(n), performing global feature association among all Gaussian anchors is computationally pro- hibitive. To address this, we propose a multi-scale stable matching scheme based on an Octree hierarchical structure, which reduces the overall time complexity from O(n”) to O(n log n), thus meet- ing the efficiency requirements of expert-guided reconstruction in large-scale scenarios, as shown in Fig. 3.

Gradient Contribution Allocation. Boundary Gaussian anchors Collaboration. Dataset Configuration. EGGS is evaluated on five large-scale datasets, including one synthetic urban dataset (MatrixCity[16]), two real-world datasets (Hospital and P1 HuiTian), and two com- plex scenes (Residence and ArtSci) from the open-source Urban- Scene3D dataset[18]. MatrixCity is sampled from the SmallCity dataset, whereas Hospital and P1 HuiTian are real-world datasets collected from actual urban environments.

For a fair comparison, all models are trained with identical hyperparameter settings, which are detailed in the supplementary material.

4.2. Rendering Quality

--- Element 149 [页码: 5 | 类型: NarrativeText] ---
【元数据】:

【内容】:
EGGS achieves superior rendering performance on both the syn- thetic MatrixCity and real-world datasets through multi-expert guided optimization. As shown in Tab. | and Fig. 4, its overall reconstruction quality matches or surpasses current SOTA meth- ods, with consistently higher PSNR values up to a 5% gain on the Hospital dataset. On the Residence dataset, EGGS’s SSIM and LPIPS are slightly lower than the best results. We attribute this to the dataset’s dense residential layout, where a single viewpoint already covers abundant scene content, yielding a natural effect similar to EGGS’s experts. This observation highlights the im- portance of viewpoint coverage in large-scale reconstruction and explains the close performance between EGGS and other SOTA baselines in this case. For the MatrixCity scene, the relatively low performance of OctreeGS may partially stem from conflicts caused by using unified hyperparameter settings across all methods.

【内容】:
Table 2. Performance comparison across five scenes for Std and training time. The standard deviation (std) metric is used to evaluate the consistency of reconstruction quality across viewpoints and training time is used to evaluate the reconstruction efficiency of each algorithm. A smaller or near-one std value indicates uniform rendering quality with minimal reconstruction isolation, while a larger std implies severe viewpoint discrepancy that degrades overall scene reconstruction quality. Best results are in bold, and second-best are underlined.
